Ramon benchmark for Z3
-
Job description: mfact branch on QF_NIA_small
Job tag: mfact
Runner: lev-ripper
Z3 repo: Z3Prover/z3
Z3 commit: 66166c5b3c7fdd17a1b4692edd7f728e303d6ad5
Z3 branch: mfact
Z3 options: "-T:60 smt.random_seed=31"
Z3 inputs: inputs/QF_NIA_small
Z3 commit message: Fix crash: use factor_core instead of factor_sqf_pp on Hensel-lifted factors

The Hensel-lifted factors may not satisfy the preconditions of
factor_sqf_pp (primitive, square-free). Use factor_core which handles
content extraction and square-free decomposition safely.

This fixes segfaults (rc=139) and aborts (rc=134) observed in the
QF_NIA_small benchmark run under ramon.

Co-authored-by: Copilot <223556219+Copilot@users.noreply.github.com>

</pre>
